Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) blue present. (B) brown present. (C) white present.
The correct answer is (B) brown present. 

Let's track the gift swaps:

1. Claire and Alice swap gifts: 
   - Claire now has the blue present.
   - Alice now has the white present.
   - Bob still has the brown present.

2. Bob and Claire swap gifts:
   - Claire now has the brown present.
   - Alice still has the white present.
   - Bob now has the blue present.

3. Alice and Bob swap gifts:
   - Claire still has the brown present.
   - Alice now has the blue present.
   - Bob now has the white present.

Therefore, at the end of the event, Claire has the brown present.

Finally, after Alice and Bob switch partners, Alice is dancing with Ophelia, Bob is dancing with Lola, and Claire is dancing with Izzi. 

Therefore, at the end of the dance, Claire is dancing with Lola. 

The correct answer is (B) Lola.

At the end of the match, Claire is playing the position that Alice started in, which is the center midfielder position. Therefore, the correct answer is (A) center midfielder.

30st data
Alice, Bob, and Claire are playing a game. At the start of the game, they are each holding a ball: Alice has a white ball, Bob has a yellow ball, and Claire has a brown ball. 

As the game progresses, pairs of players trade balls. First, Claire and Bob swap balls. Then, Alice and Claire swap balls. Finally, Bob and Claire swap balls. At the end of the game, Alice has the 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) white ball. (B) yellow ball. (C) brown ball.
The correct answer is (C) brown ball. 

Let's track the ball swaps:

1. Claire and Bob swap balls: 
   - Claire now has the yellow ball.
   - Bob now has the brown ball.
   - Alice still has the white ball.

2. Alice and Claire swap balls:
   - Alice now has the brown ball.
   - Claire now has the white ball.
   - Bob still has the yellow ball.

3. Bob and Claire swap balls:
   - Bob now has the white ball.
   - Claire now has the yellow ball.
   - Alice still has the brown ball.

Therefore, at the end of the game, Alice has the brown ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) brown ball.
pred_before : (C) brown ball.
pred_after : C
pred : C
GT : B

Finally, Alice and Bob switch partners again. After this switch, Alice is dancing with Melissa and Bob is dancing with Patrick. Claire is still dancing with Karl.

Therefore, at the end of the dance, Claire is dancing with Karl.

After Claire and Alice swap books, Claire now has The Odyssey, Alice has The Pearl, and Bob still has Frankenstein.

Therefore, at the end of the semester, Claire has Frankenstein.

Alice, Bob, and Claire are playing a game. At the start of the game, they are each holding a ball: Alice has a green ball, Bob has a blue ball, and Claire has a brown ball. 

As the game progresses, pairs of players trade balls. First, Claire and Bob swap balls. Then, Alice and Claire swap balls. Finally, Alice and Bob swap balls. At the end of the game, Alice has the 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) green ball. (B) blue ball. (C) brown ball.
The correct answer is (B) blue ball. 

Let's track the ball swaps:

1. Claire and Bob swap balls: 
   - Alice has the green ball.
   - Bob now has the brown ball.
   - Claire now has the blue ball.

2. Alice and Claire swap balls:
   - Alice now has the blue ball.
   - Bob still has the brown ball.
   - Claire now has the green ball.

3. Alice and Bob swap balls:
   - Alice now has the brown ball.
   - Bob now has the blue ball.
   - Claire still has the green ball.

Therefore, at the end of the game, Alice has the blue ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) blue ball.
pred_before : (B) blue ball.
pred_after : B
pred : B
GT : C

Alice, Bob, and Claire are on the same team in a soccer match. At the start of the match, they are each assigned to a position: Alice is playing left midfielder, Bob is playing right midfielder, and Claire is playing goalkeeper. 

As the game progresses, pairs of players occasionally swap positions. First, Bob and Alice trade positions. Then, Alice and Claire trade positions. Finally, Bob and Alice trade positions. At the end of the match, Alice is playing 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) left midfielder. (B) right midfielder. (C) goalkeeper.
At the start of the match, Alice is playing left midfielder, Bob is playing right midfielder, and Claire is playing goalkeeper. 

First, Bob and Alice trade positions. This means that Alice is now playing right midfielder and Bob is playing left midfielder. Claire remains in the goalkeeper position.

Then, Alice and Claire trade positions. Alice, who was playing right midfielder, is now the goalkeeper. Claire, who was the goalkeeper, is now playing right midfielder. Bob remains in the left midfielder position.

Finally, Bob and Alice trade positions again. Alice, who was the goalkeeper, is now playing left midfielder. Bob, who was the left midfielder, is now the goalkeeper. Claire remains in the right midfielder position.

Therefore, at the end of the match, Alice is playing left midfielder. 

The correct answer is (A) left midfielder.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) left midfielder.

After Alice and Bob swap books, Alice has Ulysses and Bob has The Odyssey.

Finally, after Alice and Bob swap books again, Alice has The Odyssey and Bob has Ulysses. 

Therefore, at the end of the semester, Bob has Ulysses.

Therefore, at the end of the dance, Alice is dancing with Karl.

83st data
Alice, Bob, and Claire are on the same team in a soccer match. At the start of the match, they are each assigned to a position: Alice is playing center midfielder, Bob is playing benchwarmer, and Claire is playing fullback. 

As the game progresses, pairs of players occasionally swap positions. First, Alice and Claire trade positions. Then, Alice and Bob trade positions. Finally, Alice and Claire trade positions. At the end of the match, Bob is playing 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) center midfielder. (B) benchwarmer. (C) fullback.
The correct answer is (C) fullback. 

At the start of the match, Bob is assigned as the benchwarmer, so he is not actively playing a position. Throughout the game, Alice and Claire trade positions twice, but Bob is not involved in any position swaps. 3. Bob and Claire swap balls: Alice still has the green ball, and Claire now has the white ball.

Therefore, at the end of the game, Alice has the green ball, Bob has the white ball, and Claire has the pink ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) white ball.
pred_before : (C) white ball.
pred_after : C

After the final swap, Claire and Bob trade positions. This means Alice remains in her position as fullback, Bob is now playing striker, and Claire is playing right winger. 

Therefore, at the end of the match, Alice is playing fullback.

   - Alice still has the orange ball.

2. Alice and Bob swap gifts:
   - Alice now has the red present.
   - Bob still has the purple present.
   - Claire still has the purple present.

3. Claire and Alice swap gifts:
   - Alice now has the red present.
   - Bob still has the purple present.
   - Claire now has the orange ball.

Therefore, at the end of the event, Alice has the red present.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) red present.

Finally, after the third swap, Alice and Claire trade positions. Alice, who was originally the left winger, swaps with Claire and becomes the left winger again. 

Therefore, at the end of the match, Alice is playing the position of left winger.

   - Alice now has The Great Gatsby, Bob has The Odyssey, and Claire has Lolita.

   - Bob gives Alice The Odyssey, and Alice gives Bob The Great Gatsby.
   - Alice now has The Odyssey, Bob has The Great Gatsby, and Claire has Lolita.

Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) Lolita.

   - Bob still has Frankenstein.

   - Alice gives Ulysses to Bob.
   - Bob gives Frankenstein to Alice.
   - Claire now has Ulysses.

At the end of the semester, Claire has Ulysses.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) Ulysses.

As the game progresses, pairs of players trade balls. First, Alice and Claire swap balls. Then, Alice and Bob swap balls. Finally, Claire and Alice swap balls. At the end of the game, Alice has the 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) purple ball. (B) red ball. (C) green ball.
The correct answer is (C) green ball. 

Let's track the ball swaps:

1. Alice and Claire swap balls: Alice now has a green ball, Bob has a red ball, and Claire has a purple ball.
2. Alice and Bob swap balls: Alice now has a red ball, Bob has a green ball, and Claire still has a purple ball.
3. Claire and Alice swap balls: Alice now has a purple ball, Bob still has a green ball, and Claire now has a red ball.

Therefore, at the end of the game, Alice has the purple ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) purple ball.
pred_before : (A) purple ball.
pred_after : A
pred : A
GT : A

219st data
Alice, Bob, and Claire are friends and avid readers who occasionally trade books. At the start of the semester, they each buy one new book: Alice gets Hound of the Baskervilles, Bob gets Catch-22, and Claire gets Ulysses. 

As the semester proceeds, they start trading around the new books. First, Bob and Claire swap books. Then, Claire and Alice swap books. Finally, Alice and Bob swap books. At the end of the semester, Alice has 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Hound of the Baskervilles. (B) Catch-22. (C) Ulysses.
The correct answer is (B) Catch-22. 

Let's track the book swaps:

1. Bob and Claire swap books: 
   - Bob gives Catch-22 to Claire.
   - Claire gives Ulysses to Bob.
   - Alice still has Hound of the Baskervilles.

2. Claire and Alice swap books:
   - Claire gives Ulysses to Alice.
   - Alice gives Hound of the Baskervilles to Claire.
   - Bob still has Catch-22.

3. Alice and Bob swap books:
   - Alice gives Hound of the Baskervilles to Bob.
   - Bob gives Catch-22 to Alice.
   - Claire still has Ulysses.

At the end of the semester, Alice has Catch-22.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) Catch-22.
pred_before : (B) Catch-22.
pred_after : B
pred : B
GT : C

Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Lolita. (B) Hound of the Baskervilles. (C) The Fellowship of the Ring.
The correct answer is (A) Lolita.

1. Claire and Bob swap books: Claire gives Bob The Fellowship of the Ring, and Bob gives Claire Hound of the Baskervilles.
   - Alice still has Lolita.
   - Bob now has Hound of the Baskervilles.
   - Claire now has The Fellowship of the Ring.

2. Alice and Bob swap books: Alice gives Bob Lolita, and Bob gives Alice Hound of the Baskervilles.
   - Alice now has Hound of the Baskervilles.
   - Bob now has Lolita.
   - Claire still has The Fellowship of the Ring.

3. Claire and Bob swap books: Claire gives Bob The Fellowship of the Ring, and Bob gives Claire Lolita.
   - Alice still has Hound of the Baskervilles.
   - Bob now has Lolita.
   - Claire now has The Fellowship of the Ring.

Therefore, at the end of the semester, Bob has Lolita.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) Lolita.

Throughout the song, the dancers often trade partners. First, Bob and Claire switch partners. Then, Claire and Alice switch partners. Finally, Bob and Alice switch partners. At the end of the dance, Claire is dancing with 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Melissa. (B) Lola. (C) Patrick.
At the end of the dance, Claire is dancing with Patrick. 

Explanation: 
At the start, Alice is dancing with Melissa, Bob is dancing with Lola, and Claire is dancing with Patrick. 

First, Bob and Claire switch partners. Now Alice is dancing with Melissa, Bob is dancing with Patrick, and Claire is dancing with Lola. 

Then, Claire and Alice switch partners. Now Alice is dancing with Lola, Bob is dancing with Patrick, and Claire is dancing with Melissa. 

Finally, Bob and Alice switch partners. Now Alice is dancing with Patrick, Bob is dancing with Melissa, and Claire is dancing with Lola. 

Therefore, at the end of the dance, Claire is dancing with Patrick. 

The correct answer is (C) Patrick.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) Patrick.
pred_before : (C) Patrick.

Alice, Bob, and Claire are holding a white elephant gift exchange. At the start of the event, they are each holding a present of a different color: Alice has a orange ball, Bob has a green present, and Claire has a red present. 

As the event progresses, pairs of people swap gifts. First, Bob and Alice swap their gifts. Then, Bob and Claire swap their gifts. Finally, Alice and Claire swap their gifts. At the end of the event, Alice has the 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) orange ball. (B) green present. (C) red present.
The correct answer is (B) green present.

After the second swap between Bob and Claire, Bob will have the red present and Claire will have the orange ball. 

After the final swap between Alice and Claire, Alice will have the red present and Claire will have the green present. 

Therefore, at the end of the event, Alice has the green present.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) green present.

1. Bob and Alice swap balls: Alice now has the blue ball and Bob has the brown ball.
2. Claire and Alice swap balls: Claire now has the blue ball and Bob still has the brown ball.
3. Bob and Claire swap balls: Claire now has the brown ball and Bob has the blue ball.

Therefore, at the end of the game, Claire has the brown ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) brown ball.

Alice, Bob, and Claire are on the same team in a soccer match. At the start of the match, they are each assigned to a position: Alice is playing left winger, Bob is playing cheerleader, and Claire is playing benchwarmer. 

As the game progresses, pairs of players occasionally swap positions. First, Bob and Alice trade positions. Then, Bob and Claire trade positions. Finally, Alice and Claire trade positions. At the end of the match, Bob is playing 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) left winger. (B) cheerleader. (C) benchwarmer.
The correct answer is (A) left winger. 

At the start of the match, Bob is assigned as the cheerleader, so he is not playing any position on the field. 

When Bob and Alice trade positions, Bob becomes the left winger and Alice becomes the cheerleader. 

When Bob and Claire trade positions, Bob remains the left winger and Claire becomes the cheerleader. 

When Alice and Claire trade positions, Alice becomes the benchwarmer and Claire becomes the left winger. 

Therefore, at the end of the match, Bob is playing the position of the left winger.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) left winger.

Then, Alice and Claire trade positions, so Alice becomes the fullback and Claire becomes the right midfielder. 

Finally, Bob and Claire trade positions, so Bob becomes the fullback and Claire becomes the right winger. 

Therefore, at the end of the match, Alice is playing fullback.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) fullback.
pred_before : (C) fullback.
pred_after : C

351st data
Alice, Bob, and Claire are friends and avid readers who occasionally trade books. At the start of the semester, they each buy one new book: Alice gets Lolita, Bob gets Hound of the Baskervilles, and Claire gets The Fellowship of the Ring. 

As the semester proceeds, they start trading around the new books. First, Claire and Bob swap books. Then, Alice and Bob swap books. Finally, Claire and Bob swap books. At the end of the semester, Alice has 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Lolita. (B) Hound of the Baskervilles. (C) The Fellowship of the Ring.
The correct answer is (B) Hound of the Baskervilles. 

Let's track the book swaps:

1. Claire and Bob swap books: 
   - Alice has Lolita
   - Bob has The Fellowship of the Ring
   - Claire has Hound of the Baskervilles

2. Alice and Bob swap books:
   - Alice now has The Fellowship of the Ring
   - Bob now has Lolita
   - Claire still has Hound of the Baskervilles

3. Claire and Bob swap books again:
   - Alice still has The Fellowship of the Ring
   - Bob now has Hound of the Baskervilles
   - Claire now has Lolita

Therefore, at the end of the semester, Alice has The Fellowship of the Ring, not Lolita.

Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) right midfielder. (B) goalkeeper. (C) left winger.

1. Claire and Bob trade positions: Alice (right midfielder), Claire (goalkeeper), Bob (left winger).
2. Bob and Alice trade positions: Alice (goalkeeper), Claire (right midfielder), Bob (left winger).
3. Claire and Bob trade positions: Alice (goalkeeper), Claire (left winger), Bob (right midfielder).

Therefore, at the end of the match, Alice is playing as the goalkeeper. 

The correct answer is (B) goalkeeper.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) goalkeeper.
pred_before : (B) goalkeeper.
pred_after : B
pred : B

As the semester proceeds, they start trading around the new books. First, Bob and Claire swap books. Then, Alice and Bob swap books. Finally, Alice and Claire swap books. At the end of the semester, Alice has 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Hound of the Baskervilles. (B) Frankenstein. (C) The Odyssey.
The correct answer is (B) Frankenstein.

Let's track the book swaps:

1. Bob and Claire swap books:
   - Alice has Hound of the Baskervilles
   - Bob has The Odyssey
   - Claire has Frankenstein

2. Alice and Bob swap books:
   - Alice now has The Odyssey
   - Bob now has Hound of the Baskervilles
   - Claire still has Frankenstein

3. Alice and Claire swap books:
   - Alice now has Frankenstein
   - Bob still has Hound of the Baskervilles
   - Claire now has The Odyssey

Therefore, at the end of the semester, Alice has Frankenstein.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) Frankenstein.
pred_before : (B) Frankenstein.
pred_after : B
pred : B
GT : B

As the game progresses, pairs of players occasionally swap positions. First, Alice and Claire trade positions. Then, Alice and Bob trade positions. Finally, Claire and Alice trade positions. At the end of the match, Alice is playing 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) goalkeeper. (B) left winger. (C) left midfielder.

After Alice and Bob trade positions, Alice becomes the left winger and Bob becomes the left midfielder. 

Finally, after Claire and Alice trade positions again, Alice becomes the goalkeeper and Claire becomes the left winger. 

Therefore, at the end of the match, Alice is playing (A) goalkeeper.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) goalkeeper.

Alice, Bob, and Claire are friends and avid readers who occasionally trade books. At the start of the semester, they each buy one new book: Alice gets Ulysses, Bob gets Frankenstein, and Claire gets Lolita. 

As the semester proceeds, they start trading around the new books. First, Claire and Bob swap books. Then, Bob and Alice swap books. Finally, Claire and Bob swap books. At the end of the semester, Claire has 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Ulysses. (B) Frankenstein. (C) Lolita.
The correct answer is (A) Ulysses. 

Let's track the book swaps:

1. Claire and Bob swap books: Claire gives Lolita to Bob, and Bob gives Frankenstein to Claire.
2. Bob and Alice swap books: Bob gives Frankenstein to Alice, and Alice gives Ulysses to Bob.
3. Claire and Bob swap books again: Claire gives Frankenstein to Bob, and Bob gives Lolita to Claire.

At the end of the swaps, Claire has Ulysses.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) Ulysses.
pred_before : (A) Ulysses.
pred_after : A
pred : A
GT : A

514st data
Alice, Bob, and Claire are dancers at a square dance. At the start of a song, they each have a partner: Alice is dancing with Izzi, Bob is dancing with Patrick, and Claire is dancing with Ophelia. 

Throughout the song, the dancers often trade partners. First, Bob and Alice switch partners. Then, Claire and Bob switch partners. Finally, Claire and Alice switch partners. At the end of the dance, Claire is dancing with 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Izzi. (B) Patrick. (C) Ophelia.
At the end of the dance, Claire is dancing with Patrick. 

Explanation: 
At the start, Alice is dancing with Izzi, Bob is dancing with Patrick, and Claire is dancing with Ophelia. 

After Bob and Alice switch partners, Alice is dancing with Patrick and Bob is dancing with Izzi. 

After Claire and Bob switch partners, Alice is still dancing with Patrick, Bob is dancing with Ophelia, and Claire is dancing with Izzi. 

Finally, after Claire and Alice switch partners, Alice is dancing with Izzi, Bob is dancing with Ophelia, and Claire is dancing with Patrick. 

Therefore, at the end of the dance, Claire is dancing with Patrick. 

The correct answer is (B) Patrick.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) Patrick.
pred_before : (B) Patrick.
pred_after : B
pred : B
GT : B

Alice, Bob, and Claire are playing a game. At the start of the game, they are each holding a ball: Alice has a white ball, Bob has a brown ball, and Claire has a black ball. 

As the game progresses, pairs of players trade balls. First, Alice and Claire swap balls. Then, Alice and Bob swap balls. Finally, Bob and Claire swap balls. At the end of the game, Claire has the 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) white ball. (B) brown ball. (C) black ball.
The correct answer is (A) white ball. 

Let's track the ball swaps:

1. Alice and Claire swap balls: Alice now has a black ball, and Claire now has a white ball.
2. Alice and Bob swap balls: Alice now has a brown ball, and Bob now has a black ball.
3. Bob and Claire swap balls: Bob now has a white ball, and Claire now has a brown ball.

At the end of the game, Claire has a brown ball, Bob has a white ball, and Alice has a black ball. Therefore, the only option that is true is that Claire has a white ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) white ball.
pred_before : (A) white ball.

Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) blue ball. (B) white ball. (C) red ball.
The correct answer is (C) red ball. 

Let's track the ball swaps:

1. Claire and Bob swap balls: 
   - Claire now has a white ball.
   - Bob now has a red ball.
   - Alice still has a blue ball.

2. Alice and Bob swap balls: 
   - Alice now has a red ball.
   - Bob now has a blue ball.
   - Claire still has a white ball.

3. Claire and Bob swap balls again: 
   - Claire now has a blue ball.
   - Bob now has a white ball.
   - Alice still has a red ball.

Therefore, at the end of the game, Bob has the white ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) white ball.
pred_before : (B) white ball.

Alice, Bob, and Claire are holding a white elephant gift exchange. At the start of the event, they are each holding a present of a different color: Alice has a white present, Bob has a yellow present, and Claire has a orange ball. 

As the event progresses, pairs of people swap gifts. First, Bob and Claire swap their gifts. Then, Alice and Claire swap their gifts. Finally, Claire and Bob swap their gifts. At the end of the event, Alice has the 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) white present. (B) yellow present. (C) orange ball.
The correct answer is (C) orange ball. 

Let's track the gift swaps:

1. Bob and Claire swap gifts: 
   - Alice has the white present.
   - Bob has the orange ball.
   - Claire has the yellow present.

2. Alice and Claire swap gifts: 
   - Alice now has the orange ball.
   - Bob still has the orange ball.
   - Claire now has the white present.

3. Claire and Bob swap gifts: 
   - Alice still has the orange ball.
   - Bob now has the white present.
   - Claire now has the orange ball.

Therefore, at the end of the event, Alice has the orange ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) orange ball.
pred_before : (C) orange ball.
pred_after : C
pred : C

After the first swap, Bob and Alice trade positions. This means Alice becomes the cheerleader and Bob becomes the goalkeeper. Claire remains as the center midfielder. 

After the second swap, Alice and Claire trade positions. Alice becomes the center midfielder and Claire becomes the cheerleader. Bob remains as the goalkeeper. 

Finally, after the third swap, Alice and Bob trade positions. Alice becomes the goalkeeper and Bob becomes the center midfielder. Claire remains as the cheerleader. 

Therefore, at the end of the match, Alice is playing as the center midfielder.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) center midfielder.

   - Claire gives The Odyssey to Alice.
   - Claire now has Hound of the Baskervilles.

Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) orange ball. (B) white ball. (C) purple ball.
The correct answer is (C) purple ball. 

At the start of the game, Alice has an orange ball, Bob has a white ball, and Claire has a purple ball. 

After the first trade, Bob and Claire swap balls. So, Alice still has the orange ball, Bob now has the purple ball, and Claire now has the white ball. 

After the second trade, Alice and Bob swap balls. So, Alice now has the purple ball, Bob now has the orange ball, and Claire still has the white ball. 

After the final trade, Claire and Bob swap balls. So, Alice still has the purple ball, Bob now has the white ball, and Claire now has the orange ball. 

Therefore, at the end of the game, Claire has the purple ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) purple ball.
pred_before : (C) purple ball.
pred_after : C
pred : C
GT : A

Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Ulysses. (B) Moby Dick. (C) Frankenstein.

1. Bob and Alice swap books: Alice now has Moby Dick and Bob has Ulysses.
2. Bob and Claire swap books: Claire now has Ulysses and Bob has Frankenstein.

Throughout the song, the dancers often trade partners. First, Claire and Bob switch partners. Then, Bob and Alice switch partners. Finally, Claire and Alice switch partners. At the end of the dance, Bob is dancing with 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Rodrigo. (B) Sam. (C) Lola.
At the end of the dance, Bob is dancing with Lola. 

Explanation: 
- At the start, Alice is dancing with Rodrigo, Bob is dancing with Sam, and Claire is dancing with Lola.
- Claire and Bob switch partners, so now Alice is dancing with Rodrigo, Bob is dancing with Lola, and Claire is dancing with Sam.
- Bob and Alice switch partners, so now Alice is dancing with Lola, Bob is dancing with Rodrigo, and Claire is dancing with Sam.
- Claire and Alice switch partners, so now Alice is dancing with Sam, Bob is dancing with Rodrigo, and Claire is dancing with Lola.

Therefore, at the end of the dance, Bob is dancing with Lola. The correct answer is (C) Lola.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) Lola.
pred_before : (C) Lola.
pred_after : C
pred : C
GT : A

Alice, Bob, and Claire are holding a white elephant gift exchange. At the start of the event, they are each holding a present of a different color: Alice has a black ball, Bob has a green present, and Claire has a orange ball. 

As the event progresses, pairs of people swap gifts. First, Alice and Bob swap their gifts. Then, Bob and Claire swap their gifts. Finally, Claire and Alice swap their gifts. At the end of the event, Claire has the 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) black ball. (B) green present. (C) orange ball.
The correct answer is (B) green present. 

After the first swap between Alice and Bob, Alice will have the green present and Bob will have the black ball. 

After the second swap between Bob and Claire, Bob will have the orange ball and Claire will have the green present. 

After the final swap between Claire and Alice, Claire will have the black ball and Alice will have the green present.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) green present.
pred_before : (B) green present.
pred_after : B
pred : B
GT : B

Alice, Bob, and Claire are playing a game. At the start of the game, they are each holding a ball: Alice has a white ball, Bob has a purple ball, and Claire has a pink ball. 

As the game progresses, pairs of players trade balls. First, Bob and Alice swap balls. Then, Bob and Claire swap balls. Finally, Bob and Alice swap balls. At the end of the game, Bob has the 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) white ball. (B) purple ball. (C) pink ball.
The correct answer is (C) pink ball. 

Let's track the ball swaps:

1. Bob and Alice swap balls: Alice now has the purple ball and Bob has the white ball.
2. Bob and Claire swap balls: Claire now has the white ball and Bob has the pink ball.
3. Bob and Alice swap balls again: Alice now has the pink ball and Bob has the white ball.

Therefore, at the end of the game, Bob has the white ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) purple ball.
pred_before : (B) purple ball.
pred_after : B

   - Bob still has a brown ball.

3. Bob and Claire swap balls:
   - Claire still has a white ball.
   - Bob now has a white ball.
   - Alice still has a yellow ball.

Therefore, at the end of the game, Claire has the white ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) white ball.

Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Hound of the Baskervilles. (B) The Pearl. (C) The Odyssey.

1. Bob and Claire swap books: Bob gives away The Pearl and receives The Odyssey.
2. Claire and Alice swap books: Claire gives away The Odyssey and receives Hound of the Baskervilles.
3. Bob and Alice swap books: Bob gives away The Odyssey and receives Hound of the Baskervilles.

Therefore, at the end of the semester, Bob has Hound of the Baskervilles.

Throughout the song, the dancers often trade partners. First, Claire and Alice switch partners. Then, Bob and Alice switch partners. Finally, Claire and Bob switch partners. At the end of the dance, Bob is dancing with 
Which choice is true ? Answer Choices: (A) Sam. (B) Helga. (C) Karl.

First, Claire and Alice switch partners. Now Alice is dancing with Karl and Claire is dancing with Sam. Bob is still dancing with Helga.

Then, Bob and Alice switch partners. Now Alice is dancing with Helga and Bob is dancing with Karl. Claire is still dancing with Sam.

Finally, Claire and Bob switch partners. Now Bob is dancing with Sam and Claire is dancing with Karl. Alice is still dancing with Helga.

Therefore, at the end of the dance, Bob is dancing with Sam.

The correct answer is (A) Sam.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) Sam.
pred_before : (A) Sam.
pred_after : A
pred : A
GT : A

At the start of the match, Alice is assigned as the cheerleader, Bob is the benchwarmer, and Claire is the left winger. 

After the first swap, Claire and Bob trade positions. This means Claire becomes the benchwarmer and Bob becomes the left winger. Alice remains the cheerleader. 

After the second swap, Claire and Alice trade positions. Claire becomes the cheerleader and Alice becomes the benchwarmer. Bob remains the left winger. 

After the final swap, Claire and Bob trade positions again. Claire becomes the left winger and Bob becomes the benchwarmer. Alice remains the cheerleader. 

Therefore, at the end of the match, Alice is still the cheerleader.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(A) cheerleader.
pred_before : (A) cheerleader.
pred_after : A

The correct answer is (B) Ulysses. 

At the start of the semester, Alice has The Great Gatsby, Bob has Ulysses, and Claire has Moby Dick. 

After Alice and Claire swap books, Alice has Moby Dick and Claire has The Great Gatsby. 

After Bob and Claire swap books, Alice still has Moby Dick, Bob has The Great Gatsby, and Claire has Ulysses. 

Finally, after Alice and Claire swap books again, Alice ends up with Ulysses, Bob has Moby Dick, and Claire has The Great Gatsby.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(B) Ulysses.

Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) Lolita.

   - Claire now has the yellow present.
   - Alice still has the white present.

   - Bob still has the orange ball.
   - Claire now has the white present.
   - Alice now has the yellow present.

3. Claire and Bob swap gifts:
   - Bob still has the orange ball.
   - Claire now has the yellow present.
   - Alice now has the white present.

Therefore, at the end of the event, Bob still has the orange ball.
Therefore, among A through C, the answer is(C) orange ball.
